\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Determine Vector of boundary conditions along the element's boundary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{  /// (or vertex) bound (S/W/N/E/SW/SE/NW/NE).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{  /// This function assumes that the same boundary condition is applied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{  /// along the entire length of an element's edge (of course, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00134}00134 \textcolor{comment}{  /// vertices combine the boundary conditions of their two adjacent edges}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00135}00135 \textcolor{comment}{  /// in the most restrictive combination. Hence, if we're at a vertex,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00136}00136 \textcolor{comment}{  /// we apply the most restrictive boundary condition of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00137}00137 \textcolor{comment}{  /// two adjacent edges. If we're on an edge (in its proper interior),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00138}00138 \textcolor{comment}{  /// we apply the least restrictive boundary condition of all nodes}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00614}00614   \textcolor{comment}{//==================================================================}\textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00615}00615 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Build the element by doing the following:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00616}00616 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ Give it nodal positions (by establishing the pointers to its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00617}00617 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   nodes)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00618}00618 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ In the process create new nodes where required (i.e. if they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00619}00619 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   don't exist in father element or have already been created}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00620}00620 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   while building new neighbour elements). Node building}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00621}00621 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   involves the following steps:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00622}00622 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Get nodal position from father element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00623}00623 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Establish the time-\/history of the newly created nodal point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00624}00624 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     (its coordinates and the previous values) consistent with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00625}00625 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     the father's history.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00626}00626 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Determine the boundary conditions of the nodes (newly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00627}00627 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     created nodes can only lie on the interior of any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00628}00628 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     edges of the father element -\/-\/ this makes it possible to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00629}00629 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     to figure out what their bc should be...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00630}00630 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Add node to the mesh's stoarge scheme for the boundary nodes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00631}00631 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Add the new node to the mesh itself}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00632}00632 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   -\/ Doc newly created nodes in "{}new\_nodes.dat"{} stored in the directory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00633}00633 \textcolor{comment}{  ///     of the DocInfo object (only if it's open!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00634}00634 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ Finally, excute the element-\/specific further\_build()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00635}00635 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   (empty by default -\/-\/ must be overloaded for specific elements).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00636}00636 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   This deals with any build operations that are not included}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00637}00637 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   in the generic process outlined above. For instance, in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00638}00638 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   Crouzeix Raviart elements we need to initialise the internal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00639}00639 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   pressure values in manner consistent with the pressure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00640}00640 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   distribution in the father element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00641}00641 \textcolor{comment}{}  \textcolor{comment}{//==================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{refineable__quad__element_8cc_source_l00642}\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1RefineableQElement_3_012_01_4_a1226bff1b077a092766cedc2a12a350f}{00642}}   \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} \mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1RefineableQElement}{RefineableQElement<2>::build}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{classoomph_1_1Mesh}{Mesh}}*\& mesh\_pt,}
